Truffles au Framboises / Raspberry Truffles

Plats: Collation/Snack
Catégories: Chocolat/Chocolate, Framboise/Raspberry
Les collections:
Source: https://www.thesumofallsweets.com/3-ingredient-white-chocolate-raspberry-truffles/
Taille de portion: 6 people
Temps de préparation: 15 mins
Temps de cuisson:

Ingrédients

200 g de chocolat blanc - 200 g white chocolate

50 g de crème à cuisson 35% - 50 g heavy cream

10 g de framboises lyophilisées - 10 g freeze dried raspberries

framboises lyophilisées supplémentaires pour l'enrobage - additional freeze dried raspberries for coating

Préparation

Hacher le chocolat blanc en petits morceaux.

Chop white chocolate into small pieces.

Au micro-ondes, chauffer la crème jusqu'à ce qu'elle soit chaude. Ne pas faire bouillir ! Verser la crème chaude sur le chocolat et laisser reposer quelques minutes.

In microwave, heat cream until hot. Do not boil! Pour hot cream over chocolate and let sit for a few minutes.

Ajouter la poudre de fruits et mélanger jusqu'à ce que le tout soit bien mélangé. Utilisez plus de poudre pour une saveur de framboise plus forte et une couleur plus profonde.

Add in the fruit powder and mix until well combined. Use more powder for a stronger raspberry flavor and deeper color.

Si nécessaire, passer au micro-ondes toutes les 5 secondes jusqu'à ce qu'il soit complètement fondu et lisse.

If needed, microwave in 5 second intervals until fully melted and smooth.

Déposez de petites boules sur une plaque de cuisson recouverte de parchemin et laissez refroidir.

Scoop small balls onto lined sheet pan, and let cool.

Roulez chaque boule entre la paume de vos mains jusqu'à consistance lisse.

Roll each ball between the palm of your hands until smooth.

Rouler chaque boule formée dans le reste de la poudre de fruits jusqu'à ce qu'elle soit complètement enrobée. Mélanger doucement entre les doigts pour secouer l'excès de poudre. Rouler quelques fois de plus pour s'assurer que la poudre est bien attachée au chocolat.

Roll each formed ball in remaining fruit powder until completely coated. Toss gently between fingers to shake off extra powder. Roll a couple more times to ensure powder is fully attached to chocolate.

Servir à température ambiante.

Serve at room temperature.

Cholestérol: 18mg
Sodium: 33mg
Glucides totaux: 20g

Tzatziki

Plats: Accompagnement/Side Dish
Catégories: Ail/Garlic, Concombre/Cucumber, Sauce, Yaourt/Yogurt
Les collections:
Source: https://cookieandkate.com/how-to-make-tzatziki/
Taille de portion: 2 1/2 tasse/cups
Temps de préparation: 15 mins
Temps de cuisson:

Ingrédients

2 tasses de concombre râpé - 2 cups grated cucumber

1½ tasses de yaourt grec nature - 1½ cups plain Greek yogurt

2 cuillères à soupe d'huile d'olive extra vierge - 2 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil

2 cuillères à soupe de menthe fraîche hachée et/ou d'aneth - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh mint and/or dill

1 cuillère à soupe de jus de citron - 1 tablespoon lemon juice

1 gousse d'ail moyenne, pressée ou hachée - 1 medium clove garlic, pressed or minced

¼ cuillère à thé de sel - ¼ teaspoon salt

Préparation

En travaillant avec une grosse poignée à la fois, pressez légèrement le concombre râpé entre vos paumes au-dessus de l'évier pour éliminer l'excès d'humidité. Transférer le concombre pressé dans un bol de service et répéter avec le concombre restant.

Working with one big handful at a time, lightly squeeze the grated cucumber between your palms over the sink to remove excess moisture. Transfer the squeezed cucumber to a serving bowl, and repeat with the remaining cucumber.

Ajouter le yaourt, l'huile d'olive, les herbes, le jus de citron, l'ail et le sel dans le bol et remuer pour mélanger. Laisser reposer le mélange pendant 5 minutes pour permettre aux saveurs de se marier. Add the yogurt, olive oil, herbs, lemon juice, garlic, and salt to the bowl, and stir to blend. Let the mixture rest for 5 minutes to allow the flavors to meld.

Servir le tzatziki immédiatement ou réfrigérer pour plus tard. Les restes de tzatziki se conservent bien, au frais, pendant environ 4 jours.

Serve tzatziki immediately or chill for later. Leftover tzatziki keeps well, chilled, for about 4 days.

Nutrition

Upgraded German Chocolate Cake

Plats: Déssert/Dessert
Catégories: Chocolat/Chocolate, Gâteau/Cake, Noix de Coco/Coconut, Pacane/Pecan
Les collections: À nettoyer/To Clean
Source: https://sallysbakingaddiction.com/german-chocolate-cake/
Taille de portion: serves 10-12; 2.5 cups filling
Temps de préparation: 45 mins
Temps de cuisson: 35 mins

Ingrédients

1 and 3/4 cups (219g) all-purpose flour (spooned & leveled)

3/4 cup (62g) unsweetened natural cocoa powder

1 and 3/4 cups (350g) granulated sugar

2 teaspoons baking soda

1 teaspoon baking powder

1 teaspoon salt

2 teaspoons espresso powder (optional)*

1/2 cup (120ml) canola or vegetable oil

2 large eggs, at room temperature

3/4 cup (180g) full fat sour cream, at room temperature

1/2 cup (120ml) buttermilk, at room temperature*

2 teaspoons pure vanilla extract

1/2 cup (120ml) hot water or coffee*

1/2 cup (8 Tbsp; 113g) unsalted butter

1 cup (200g) packed light or dark brown sugar

3 large egg yolks

1 can (8 ounces; 240ml) evaporated milk

1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract

2 cups sweetened shredded coconut

1 cup (125g) chopped pecans

use this chocolate buttercream for a naked-style cake

use this chocolate buttercream for frosting the top and sides

optional for garnish: extra toasted pecans and sweetened shredded coconut

Préparation

1. Preheat oven to 350°F (177°C). Grease three 9-inch round cake pans, line with parchment paper rounds, then grease the parchment paper. Parchment paper helps the cakes seamlessly release from the pans. (If it’s helpful, see this parchment paper rounds for cakes video & post.)

2. Whisk the flour, cocoa powder, sugar, baking soda, baking powder, salt, and espresso powder (if using) together in a large bowl. Set aside. Using a handheld or stand mixer fitted with a whisk attachment (or you can use a whisk) mix the oil, eggs, sour cream, buttermilk, and vanilla together until combined. Pour the wet ingredients into the dry ingredients, add the hot water or coffee, and whisk or beat it all until the batter is completely combined.

3. Divide batter evenly between 3 pans. Bake for 21-25 minutes. Baking times vary, so keep an eye on yours. The cakes are done when a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.

4. Remove the cakes from the oven and set on a wire rack. Allow to cool completely in the pan.

5. so it can cool and be ready at the same time. Combine butter, brown sugar, egg yolks, and evaporated milk in a medium saucepan over medium heat. Whisk occasionally as the mixture comes to a low boil. Once boiling, whisk constantly until the mixture thickens, about 5 minutes. Remove from heat and stir in vanilla, toasted pecans, and coconut. Allow to cool completely before layering in cake. It will thicken even more as it cools.

6. First, level the cakes if needed: using a large serrated knife, slice a thin layer off the tops of the cakes to create a flat surface. Discard (or crumble over ice cream!). Place 1 cake layer on your cake stand, cake turntable, or serving plate. Evenly cover the top with 1/2 of the coconut pecan filling (half is about 1 and 1/4 cups). Top with 2nd layer and evenly cover the top with remaining coconut pecan filling. Top with the third cake layer. Spread the chocolate buttercream into a thick layer on top. Garnish with extra toasted pecans and coconut, if desired. Refrigerate for at least 45 minutes before slicing or else the cake may gently fall apart as you cut.

7. Cover leftover cake tightly and store in the refrigerator for 5 days.
